********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user WHERE id = 7
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user_performance WHERE user_id = 7
********************************
Q: SELECT *, IFNULL((SELECT pgu.pond_valor FROM pond_group_user pgu WHERE pgu.pond_user = 7 AND pgu.pond_id = pg.id),0) myPond FROM pond_group pg
********************************
Q: SELECT *, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 7 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 0 WHERE materia = 1 AND id = 7
********************************
Q: SELECT *, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 7 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 2
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 514 WHERE materia = 2 AND id = 7

Q: SELECT ug.*, m.name materia_name, m.color materia_color FROM user_goal ug, materia m WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.points > 0 AND m.id = ug.materia AND m.active = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT c.* FROM user_relations ur, course c WHERE ur.user_id = 7 AND ur.course_id = c.id
********************************
Q: select * from materia where id = 2
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 2 AND e.library = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde > NOW() AND lf.library_hasta < NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde > NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 3 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde > NOW() AND lf.library_hasta < NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde > NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC

									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 7 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 5
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 0 WHERE materia = 5 AND id = 7
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 0 WHERE materia = 6 AND id = 7
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 0 WHERE materia = 7 AND id = 7
********************************
Q: UPDATE user SET ultima_ponderacion = 0, puntaje_ponderacion = 0, porc_cumplimiento = 0 WHERE id = 7
********************************
Q: SELECT ug.*, m.name materia_name, m.color materia_color FROM user_goal ug, materia m WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.points > 0 AND m.id = ug.materia AND m.active = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT c.* FROM user_relations ur, course c WHERE ur.user_id = 7 AND ur.course_id = c.id
********************************
Q: select * from materia where id = 2
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 2 AND e.library = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 16 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

Q: SELECT tr.*, 
	        c.name course_name, 
	        m.name materia_name, 
	        IFNULL((SELECT  AVG(tp.points)
	        FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
	                user_relations ur, 
	                course c1, 
	                user u 
	        WHERE  tp.materia = m.id AND 
	                tp.user_id = u.id AND 
	                ur.user_id = u.id AND 
	                ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
	                c1.id = c.id AND 
	                ur.course_id = c.id AND 
	                tp.test_id = (SELECT MAX(x1.id) FROM test x1 WHERE EXISTS(SELECT * FROM test_end_head x2 WHERE x2.test_id = x1.id AND x2.user_id = u.id) ORDER BY x1.id DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
	                tp.points > 0 AND 
	                tp.isLast = 1   
	        ),0) puntosPromedio  
	FROM  teacher_relations tr, 
	       course c, 
	       materia m 
	WHERE tr.teacher_id = 5 AND 
	      tr.course_id = c.id AND 
	      tr.materia_id = m.id
********************************

									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 11 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 2

Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 3 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC

Q: SELECT *, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 13 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 13 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1
********************************

Q: SELECT ts.user_id, 
									   (select u.name from user u where u.id = ts.user_id) user_name, 
									   COUNT(*) qty 
								FROM test_end_detail ts, 
									 user_relations ur 
								WHERE 
									ts.isOk = 1 AND 
									ts.test_id = (SELECT teh.test_id FROM test_end_head teh WHERE teh.user_id = ur.user_id AND teh.materia = 2 AND teh.isLast = 1 ORDER BY teh.cuando DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
									ts.user_id = ur.user_id AND 
									ur.course_id = 4 GROUP BY ts.user_id ORDER BY qty DESC
********************************

Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 3 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 2 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user WHERE id = 7
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user_performance WHERE user_id = 7
********************************
Q: SELECT *, IFNULL((SELECT pgu.pond_valor FROM pond_group_user pgu WHERE pgu.pond_user = 7 AND pgu.pond_id = pg.id),0) myPond FROM pond_group pg
********************************
Q: SELECT *, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 7 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 0 WHERE materia = 1 AND id = 7
********************************

									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points,

							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 2
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 514 WHERE materia = 2 AND id = 7

							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 5

Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

Q: SELECT ts.user_id, 
									   (select u.name from user u where u.id = ts.user_id) user_name, 
									   COUNT(*) qty 
								FROM test_end_detail ts, 
									 user_relations ur 
								WHERE 
									ts.isOk = 1 AND 
									ts.test_id = (SELECT teh.test_id FROM test_end_head teh WHERE teh.user_id = ur.user_id AND teh.materia = 1 AND teh.isLast = 1 ORDER BY teh.cuando DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
									ts.user_id = ur.user_id AND 
									ur.course_id = 4 GROUP BY ts.user_id ORDER BY qty DESC
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user WHERE id = 3

Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 1 AND e.library = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT ts.user_id, 
									   (select u.name from user u where u.id = ts.user_id) user_name, 
									   COUNT(*) qty 
								FROM test_end_detail ts, 
									 user_relations ur 
								WHERE 
									ts.isOk = 1 AND 
									ts.eje = 1 AND 
									ts.test_id = (SELECT teh.test_id FROM test_end_head teh WHERE teh.user_id = ur.user_id AND teh.materia = 1 AND teh.isLast = 1 ORDER BY teh.cuando DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
									ts.user_id = ur.user_id AND 
									ur.course_id = 4 GROUP BY ts.user_id ORDER BY qty DESC
********************************
Q: SELECT count(*) x, p.test_id FROM preg p, test t WHERE p.test_id = t.id AND t.customer_id = 0 AND p.eje = 1 and t.active = 1 GROUP BY p.test_id
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user WHERE id = 3
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user_performance WHERE user_id = 3
********************************
Q: INSERT INTO `user_performance` (`user_id`,`materia_id`,`eje_id`,`performance`) VALUES ('3', '1', '1', 3) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE `performance`=3
********************************
Q: SELECT ts.user_id, 
									   (select u.name from user u where u.id = ts.user_id) user_name, 
									   COUNT(*) qty 
								FROM test_end_detail ts, 
									 user_relations ur 
								WHERE 
									ts.isOk = 1 AND 
									ts.eje = 3 AND 
									ts.test_id = (SELECT teh.test_id FROM test_end_head teh WHERE teh.user_id = ur.user_id AND teh.materia = 1 AND teh.isLast = 1 ORDER BY teh.cuando DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
									ts.user_id = ur.user_id AND 
									ur.course_id = 4 GROUP BY ts.user_id ORDER BY qty DESC
********************************
Q: SELECT count(*) x, p.test_id FROM preg p, test t WHERE p.test_id = t.id AND t.customer_id = 0 AND p.eje = 3 and t.active = 1 GROUP BY p.test_id
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM user WHERE id = 3

Q: SELECT * FROM user_performance WHERE user_id = 3

Q: INSERT INTO `user_performance` (`user_id`,`materia_id`,`eje_id`,`performance`) VALUES ('3', '1', '3', 2) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE `performance`=2
********************************
Q: SELECT ts.user_id, 
									   (select u.name from user u where u.id = ts.user_id) user_name, 
									   COUNT(*) qty 
								FROM test_end_detail ts, 
									 user_relations ur 
								WHERE 
									ts.isOk = 1 AND 
									ts.eje = 14 AND 
									ts.test_id = (SELECT teh.test_id FROM test_end_head teh WHERE teh.user_id = ur.user_id AND teh.materia = 1 AND teh.isLast = 1 ORDER BY teh.cuando DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
									ts.user_id = ur.user_id AND 
									ur.course_id = 4 GROUP BY ts.user_id ORDER BY qty DESC
********************************
Q: SELECT count(*) x, p.test_id FROM preg p, test t WHERE p.test_id = t.id AND t.customer_id = 0 AND p.eje = 14 and t.active = 1 GROUP BY p.test_id
********************************

Q: SELECT * FROM user_performance WHERE user_id = 3

Q: INSERT INTO `user_performance` (`user_id`,`materia_id`,`eje_id`,`performance`) VALUES ('3', '1', '14', 3) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE `performance`=3

Q: SELECT tr.*, 
	        c.name course_name, 
	        m.name materia_name, 
	        IFNULL((SELECT  AVG(tp.points)
	        FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
	                user_relations ur, 
	                course c1, 
	                user u 
	        WHERE  tp.materia = m.id AND 
	                tp.user_id = u.id AND 
	                ur.user_id = u.id AND 
	                ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
	                c1.id = c.id AND 
	                ur.course_id = c.id AND 
	                tp.test_id = (SELECT MAX(x1.id) FROM test x1 WHERE EXISTS(SELECT * FROM test_end_head x2 WHERE x2.test_id = x1.id AND x2.user_id = u.id) ORDER BY x1.id DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
	                tp.points > 0 AND 
	                tp.isLast = 1   
	        ),0) puntosPromedio  
	FROM  teacher_relations tr, 
	       course c, 
	       materia m 
	WHERE tr.teacher_id = 5 AND 
	      tr.course_id = c.id AND 
	      tr.materia_id = m.id
********************************
Q: SELECT m.*
				  FROM teacher_relations tr, course c, materia m 
				  WHERE tr.teacher_id = 5 AND tr.course_id = c.id AND tr.materia_id = m.id AND c.id = 4
********************************
Q: SELECT ur.*, tr.goal FROM teacher_relations tr, user_relations ur WHERE tr.course_id = 4 AND tr.materia_id = 1 AND ur.course_id = tr.course_id

									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 3 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points,

							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1

Q: SELECT 	t.*, 
					        IFNULL((SELECT  AVG(tp.points)
							        FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
							                user_relations ur, 
							                course c1, 
							                user u 
							        WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
							                tp.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
							                c1.id = 4 AND 
							                ur.course_id = 4 AND 
							                tp.test_id = t.id AND 
							                tp.points > 0 AND 
							                tp.isLast = 1
							        ),0) puntosPromedio  
					FROM 	test t
					WHERE 	t.isAll = 1 AND 
							t.materia = 1
********************************

********************************
Q: SELECT tp.points
				FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
				        user_relations ur, 
				        course c1, 
				        user u 
				WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
				        tp.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
				        c1.id = 4 AND 
				        ur.course_id = 4 AND 
				        tp.test_id = 4 AND 
				        tp.points > 0 AND 
				        tp.isLast = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT e.*, 
													 m.name mname,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 4 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_preg,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 4 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND ts.isOk = 1 AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_ok_preg 
													 FROM eje e, materia m 
													 WHERE e.active = 1 AND e.parent = m.id AND m.id = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT p.*, e.name eje_name, e.id eje_id, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 1) win,
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 0) lose, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 0) A, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 1) B, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 2) C, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 3) D, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 4) E, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 5) F, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 6) G, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 7) H
																		  FROM preg p, eje e WHERE p.test_id = 4 AND p.eje = e.id ORDER BY p.orden ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 1 AND e.active = 1
********************************

Q: SELECT 	t.*, 
					        IFNULL((SELECT  AVG(tp.points)
							        FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
							                user_relations ur, 
							                course c1, 
							                user u 
							        WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
							                tp.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
							                c1.id = 4 AND 
							                ur.course_id = 4 AND 
							                tp.test_id = t.id AND 
							                tp.points > 0 AND 
							                tp.isLast = 1
							        ),0) puntosPromedio  
					FROM 	test t
					WHERE 	t.isAll = 1 AND 
							t.materia = 1
********************************

Q: SELECT * FROM test_end_head tp, user_relations ur where tp.test_id = 4 AND ur.course_id = 4 AND ur.user_id = tp.user_id AND tp.isLast = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT tp.points
				FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
				        user_relations ur, 
				        course c1, 
				        user u 
				WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
				        tp.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
				        c1.id = 4 AND 
				        ur.course_id = 4 AND 
				        tp.test_id = 4 AND 
				        tp.points > 0 AND 
				        tp.isLast = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT e.*, 
													 m.name mname,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 4 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_preg,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 4 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND ts.isOk = 1 AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_ok_preg 
													 FROM eje e, materia m 
													 WHERE e.active = 1 AND e.parent = m.id AND m.id = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT p.*, e.name eje_name, e.id eje_id, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 1) win,
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 0) lose, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 0) A, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 1) B, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 2) C, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 3) D, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 4) E, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 5) F, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 6) G, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 7) H
																		  FROM preg p, eje e WHERE p.test_id = 4 AND p.eje = e.id ORDER BY p.orden ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 1 AND e.active = 1
********************************

********************************

Q: SELECT 	t.*, 
					        IFNULL((SELECT  AVG(tp.points)
							        FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
							                user_relations ur, 
							                course c1, 
							                user u 
							        WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
							                tp.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
							                c1.id = 4 AND 
							                ur.course_id = 4 AND 
							                tp.test_id = t.id AND 
							                tp.points > 0 AND 
							                tp.isLast = 1
							        ),0) puntosPromedio  
					FROM 	test t
					WHERE 	t.isAll = 1 AND 
							t.materia = 1
********************************

********************************
Q: SELECT tp.points
				FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
				        user_relations ur, 
				        course c1, 
				        user u 
				WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
				        tp.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
				        c1.id = 4 AND 
				        ur.course_id = 4 AND 
				        tp.test_id = 4 AND 
				        tp.points > 0 AND 
				        tp.isLast = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT e.*, 
													 m.name mname,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 4 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_preg,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 4 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND ts.isOk = 1 AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_ok_preg 
													 FROM eje e, materia m 
													 WHERE e.active = 1 AND e.parent = m.id AND m.id = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT p.*, e.name eje_name, e.id eje_id, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 1) win,
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 0) lose, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 0) A, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 1) B, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 2) C, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 3) D, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 4) E, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 5) F, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 6) G, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 7) H
																		  FROM preg p, eje e WHERE p.test_id = 4 AND p.eje = e.id ORDER BY p.orden ASC
********************************

********************************

									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 12 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1

Q: SELECT 	t.*, 
					        IFNULL((SELECT  AVG(tp.points)
							        FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
							                user_relations ur, 
							                course c1, 
							                user u 
							        WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
							                tp.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.user_id = u.id AND 
							                ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
							                c1.id = 4 AND 
							                ur.course_id = 4 AND 
							                tp.test_id = t.id AND 
							                tp.points > 0 AND 
							                tp.isLast = 1
							        ),0) puntosPromedio  
					FROM 	test t
					WHERE 	t.isAll = 1 AND 
							t.materia = 1
********************************

********************************
Q: SELECT tp.points
				FROM 	test_end_head tp, 
				        user_relations ur, 
				        course c1, 
				        user u 
				WHERE  tp.materia = 1 AND 
				        tp.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.user_id = u.id AND 
				        ur.course_id = c1.id AND 
				        c1.id = 4 AND 
				        ur.course_id = 4 AND 
				        tp.test_id = 6 AND 
				        tp.points > 0 AND 
				        tp.isLast = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT e.*, 
													 m.name mname,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 6 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_preg,
													 (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = 6 AND ts.materia = m.id AND ts.eje = e.id AND ts.isOk = 1 AND EXISTS(SELECT * FROM user_relations ur WHERE ur.user_id = ts.user_id AND ur.course_id = 4)) all_ok_preg 
													 FROM eje e, materia m 
													 WHERE e.active = 1 AND e.parent = m.id AND m.id = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT p.*, e.name eje_name, e.id eje_id, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 1) win,
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.isOk = 0) lose, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 0) A, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 1) B, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 2) C, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 3) D, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 4) E, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 5) F, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 6) G, 
																		  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM test_end_detail ts WHERE ts.test_id = p.test_id AND ts.preg = p.id AND ts.reply = 7) H
																		  FROM preg p, eje e WHERE p.test_id = 6 AND p.eje = e.id ORDER BY p.orden ASC
********************************

Q: SELECT 	lf.*
								FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt 
								WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
										lt.eje_id = 1 AND lt.teacher_id = 5 AND 
										lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
										( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
										  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
										  lf.library_planificada = 0
										)
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC

Q: SELECT *, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points,

								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 15 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC

Q: SELECT m.* FROM materia m WHERE m.active = 1 AND m.superior = 0 AND EXISTS(SELECT g.* FROM teacher_relations g WHERE g.materia_id = m.id AND g.teacher_id = 5) ORDER BY m.orden ASC
********************************
Q: select * from materia where id = 2
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 2 AND e.library = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*,
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(x.rendimiento) from library_target x where x.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND x.eje_id = 13) rendimiento, 
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 13 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 13 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

Q: SELECT 	lf.*,
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(x.rendimiento) from library_target x where x.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND x.eje_id = 13) rendimiento, 
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 13 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 13 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM teacher WHERE id = 5

********************************
Q: SELECT *, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 7 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1
********************************
Q: UPDATE user_goal SET ultima_psu = 0 WHERE materia = 1 AND id = 7

Q: SELECT c.* FROM user_relations ur, course c WHERE ur.user_id = 7 AND ur.course_id = c.id
********************************
Q: select * from materia where id = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 1 AND e.library = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 1 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 1 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 3 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 1 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 2 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 7 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points, 
									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 7 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1

Q: SELECT 	lf.*, t.name teacher_name 
							FROM	library_files lf, library_target lt, teacher t 
							WHERE 	lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND 
									lt.eje_id = 13 AND 
									lt.rendimiento = 1 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR 
									  lf.library_planificada = 0
									) AND lt.course_id IN (4) 
							ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

									lt.rendimiento = 3 AND 
									lf.teacher_id = t.id AND 
									( ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.library_hasta > NOW() ) OR 
									  ( lf.library_planificada = 1 AND lf.library_desde < NOW() AND lf.sin_termino = 1 ) OR

									 IFNULL((SELECT tp.points FROM test_end_head tp WHERE tp.isLast = 1 AND tp.materia = m.id AND tp.user_id = 12 ORDER BY cuando DESC LIMIT 1),0) ultimo_puntaje 
							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 2
********************************

Q: SELECT ts.user_id, 
									   (select u.name from user u where u.id = ts.user_id) user_name, 
									   COUNT(*) qty 
								FROM test_end_detail ts, 
									 user_relations ur 
								WHERE 
									ts.isOk = 1 AND 
									ts.test_id = (SELECT teh.test_id FROM test_end_head teh WHERE teh.user_id = ur.user_id AND teh.materia = 2 AND teh.isLast = 1 ORDER BY teh.cuando DESC LIMIT 1) AND 
									ts.user_id = ur.user_id AND 
									ur.course_id = 4 GROUP BY ts.user_id ORDER BY qty DESC
********************************

Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 1 AND e.library = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*,
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(x.rendimiento) from library_target x where x.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND x.eje_id = 1) rendimiento, 
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 1 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 1 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

Q: SELECT 	lf.*,
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(x.rendimiento) from library_target x where x.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND x.eje_id = 13) rendimiento, 
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 13 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 13 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

Q: SELECT 	lf.*,
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(x.rendimiento) from library_target x where x.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND x.eje_id = 1) rendimiento, 
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 1 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 1 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM teacher WHERE id = 5
********************************

										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 13 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 13 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM teacher WHERE id = 5
********************************
Q: SELECT m.* FROM materia m WHERE m.active = 1 AND m.superior = 0 AND EXISTS(SELECT g.* FROM teacher_relations g WHERE g.materia_id = m.id AND g.teacher_id = 5) ORDER BY m.orden ASC

Q: select * from materia where id = 2

								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 15 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC

Q: SELECT m.* FROM materia m WHERE m.active = 1 AND m.superior = 0 AND EXISTS(SELECT g.* FROM teacher_relations g WHERE g.materia_id = m.id AND g.teacher_id = 5) ORDER BY m.orden ASC
********************************
Q: select * from materia where id = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT * FROM eje e WHERE e.parent = 1 AND e.library = 1
********************************
Q: SELECT 	lf.*,
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(x.rendimiento) from library_target x where x.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND x.eje_id = 1) rendimiento, 
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 1 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 1 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC
********************************

								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC

Q: SELECT 	lf.*,
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT x.rendimiento) from library_target x where x.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND x.eje_id = 1) rendimiento, 
										(select GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT y1.name) from library_target y, course y1 where y.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND y.eje_id = 1 AND y.course_id=y1.id) cursos 
								FROM	library_files lf
								WHERE 	lf.teacher_id = 5 AND 
								EXISTS ( SELECT * FROM library_target lt WHERE lt.library_file_id = lf.file_id AND lt.eje_id = 1 )
								ORDER BY lf.library_name ASC

									 IFNULL((SELECT ug.points FROM user_goal ug WHERE ug.id = 3 AND ug.materia = m.id),0) points,

							FROM pond_group_materia pg, materia m 
							WHERE pg.pond_materia = m.id AND m.active = 1 AND pg.pond_id = 1
